ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　省试停，秋应京兆试，列等第，成为“十哲”之一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　在长安，落第，有诗送颜时东归。作品：《送太学颜明经及第东归》<div id='poem_39253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_39253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_39357'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_39357'>妖星沈雨露，和气满京关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_39357'>上将忠勋立，明君法驾还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_39357'>顺风调雅乐，夹道序群班。<div id='poem_sentence_2_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_39357'>香泛传宣里，尘清指顾间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_39357'>楼台新紫气，云物旧黄山。<div id='poem_sentence_4_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_39357'>晓渭行朝肃，秋郊旷望闲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_39357'>庙灵安国步，日角动天颜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_39357'>浩浩升平曲，流歌彻百蛮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_39357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_39357'></div><div 湘潭

<div class='label1' id='621daded0ae940f18358f955e0d1ca68_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("621daded0ae940f18358f955e0d1ca68");'><span id='621daded0ae940f18358f955e0d1ca68_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，更结伴南游，至湘潭，有诗。作品：《南游》<span class='inlineComment2'>（不详作于何地，暂置于此。）</span>《江上阻风》<span class='inlineComment2'>（不详作于何地，暂置于此。）</span><div id='poem_39232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_39232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_39232'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_39232'>凄凉怀古意，湘浦吊灵均。<div id='poem_sentence_0_39232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_39232'>故国经新岁，扁舟寄病身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_39232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_39232'>山城多晓瘴，泽国少晴春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_39232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_39232'>渐远无相识，青梅独向<span id='poem_sentence_2_39377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_39377'>鬓秃又惊逢献岁，眼前浑不见交亲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_39377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_39377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_39377_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c85b6fbef55b41d9842630512502416b_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=887&endYear=887')">887年</a>，40岁</div><div id='c85b6fbef55b41d9842630512502416b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=887&endYear=887')">887年</a>　僖宗在兴元。二月，谷进士及第。<br /></div>
-----end

class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_39284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/39284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄同年礼部赵郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（893年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20907, "唐末", "郑谷", "poem_title_39284")'>郑谷</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_39284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_39284'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_39284'>仙步徐徐整<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_39284", 39284, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>羽衣</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_39284", 39284, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>小仪</span>澄澹转<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_39284", 39284, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>中仪</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_39284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_39284'>桦<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作花）</span>飘红烬趋朝路，兰纵清香宿省时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_39284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_39284'>彩笔烟霞供不足，纶<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作粉）</span>闱鸾凤讶来迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_39284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_39284'>自怜孤宦谁相念，祷祝空吟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作凭）</span>一首诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_39284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_39284'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_39284_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='22e09c27c7fe4ce18a2fdd4670713b2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("22e09c27c7fe4ce18a2fdd4670713b2f");'><span id='22e09c27c7fe4ce18a2fdd4670713b2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=894&endYear=894')">894年</a>，47岁</div><div id='22e09c27c7fe4ce18a2fdd4670713b2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=894&endYear=894')">894年</a>　返京途中，经过南阳，有诗。作品：《再经南阳》<div id='poem_39090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_39090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/39090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再经南阳</a><span class='authorDate'>（894年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20907, "唐末", "郑谷", "poem_title_39090")'>郑谷</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_39090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_39090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_39090'>平芜漠漠失楼台，昔日游人乱后来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_39090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_39090'>寥落<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_39090", 39090, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>墙匡</span>春欲暮，烧残宫树有花开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_39090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_39090'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_39090_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
武昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7aa3d59e55144388933d84ae5a7f769b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7aa3d59e55144388933d84ae5a7f769b");'><span id='7aa3d59e55144388933d84ae5a7f769b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>，57岁</div><div id='7aa3d59e55144388933d84ae5a7f769b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　僧虚中恰于此时献诗劝退。谷志遂决，乘乱弃官归宜春。辗转奔匿，至夏口，已九月残，惊魂稍定，有诗。作品：《重阳夜旅怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作于何地难定，暂置于此。）</span><div id='poem_39125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_39125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/39125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重阳夜旅怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（904年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(20907, "唐末", "郑谷", "poem_title_39125")'>郑谷</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_39125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_39125'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_39125'>强插黄花三两枝，还图一醉浸愁眉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_39125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_39125'>半床斜月醉醒后，惆怅多于未醉时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_39125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_39125'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_39125_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
